msg:I chose this hotel because I saw a lot of recommendations, but I think the ones I wrote are not objective enough. The advantages are obvious. You can walk a few steps to the beach, and the sand is not as fine as that of the Stone Man. There is a large barrel slide in front of the hotel, which is suitable for older babies. Go a little further and there is a playground by the sea, where the baby can play. There is a 1903 Time Brewing Workshop next to the hotel, which is convenient for eating. There are Chinese and Western food inside, 100 per person, good environment, and good taste. There is also a bakery, the young lady inside is very enthusiastic, and the bread is also great. Now let's talk about the shortcomings. The hotel staff is obviously not enough. We two mothers brought two 22-month-old babies to check in. On the day of check-in, the babies fell asleep on their mothers' shoulders. After getting off the car, each dragged a large suitcase and a backpack. There was no service staff at the door. I went in and asked the front desk staff to come out to take the luggage. The bed guard in the room was not installed correctly. I called the staff to help adjust it, and then two aunts in casual clothes came. The aunt said they were about to get off work. We borrowed sand dredging tools and asked for a bag to put it in. The front desk lady said that the bag was used up. The night light in my room was broken, the sink in my friend's room was leaking, and the bed was very loose. We didn't sleep well and hugged the baby all night. The items in the room were all within the reach of the child, and there were a lot of small things. The shelf next to the bathtub could be pushed around. The soundproofing of the room was also average. The baby in the next room was crying, and I could hear the door of the room outside closing and opening. Of course, the hardware facilities of the hotel are all good. The room is newly decorated, and the toiletries and hair dryers inside are very good. There are Xiaodu, Xiaomi appliances, etc. Although there are not many breakfasts in the hotel, they are all delicious, and there are various categories, which are few but good. To be honest, my friend and I were not very satisfied after checking in. Later, after dinner, we pushed the baby (the stroller was provided by the hotel, very new and smooth) for a walk on the beach, looking at the scenery of the beach, and thought it was not bad, but it was windy and rainy that night, and I didn't sleep well all night. The next day, there was also a level 5 gale at the beach. It was not suitable for the baby to dig sand at the beach, nor to go to the playground at the beach to play, so we decided to check out early and return to the original hotel in Shinan District. When we checked out, we were given a few bubble toys. Also, the price is five-star, but it feels more like a high-end portable hotel. The hotel staff is small and lacks professional training. There is no proactive service, but if you ask for help, they will try their best to solve it. Overall, I don‚Äôt think it‚Äôs suitable to bring a small baby into the wine barrel refrigerator magnet. The attitude is also good. This hotel says it is a five-star stay. The above is my experience of staying, I hope it can be a reference for everyone.
